salt	<h3>salt</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>盐, 食盐<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Salt occurs naturally in sea water.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 盐天然存于海水中。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is considerable salt in the kitchen.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 厨房里有相当多的盐。</font><br>味道或外观等像盐的物质; 药用盐类<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Salts is a medicine that causes movements of the bowels.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 泻盐是一种促使肠子运动的药物。</font><br>增添趣味[活跃气氛]的事物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Her witty remarks added a little salt to the conversation.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她的妙语使谈话增添了一些风趣。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Adventure is the salt of life to some men.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 对有些男子而言, 冒险是生活的乐趣。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>加盐于…以调味; 用盐腌<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I forgot to salt the dish.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这盘菜我忘记放盐了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The fish are cut and salted.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 鱼被切成块腌起来了。</font><br>撒盐于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The main roads have been salted.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 主要公路上撒了盐。</font><br>使更有趣<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He employs an irreverent humour to salt his observation.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他运用玩世不恭的幽默使他的评论更加有趣。</font><br>\n

sick	<h3>sick</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>不舒服的; 有病的, 患病的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I must inquire after my sick friend.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我得去问候我那得了病的朋友。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She's sick, but she doesn't show it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她病了, 但无病态。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He fell sick with flu.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他得了流感。</font><br>恶心的; 想吐的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He began to feel sick as soon as the ship started to move.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 船一启动他就开始呕吐。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is sick from overeating.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他因暴饮暴食而呕吐。</font><br>腻烦的, 厌恶的, 讨厌的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I feel sick at my work.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我讨厌我的工作。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I am heartily sick of them.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我深觉他们讨厌。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We are sick of your complaining.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们讨厌你抱怨。</font><br>心烦意乱的, 恼火的, 不高兴的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is sick at heart.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她心里烦闷。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was awfully sick at being beaten.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 因被击败他极不愉快。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is sick with me for being so late.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她对我来得这样迟感到不高兴。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>〈口〉呕吐物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The bed was full of sick.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 床上全是吐的东西。</font><br>\n
sigh	<h3>sigh</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>叹气, 叹息<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She sighed and looked sad.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她叹了口气, 显得很伤心。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She sighed with relief when she heard the good news.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 听到这个好消息时, 她宽慰地舒了口气。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>叹息, 叹气<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The old man gave a deep sigh.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那老人深深地叹了口气。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We all make a sigh of relief when we heard that he was safe.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 听说他平安无事, 我们都松了一口气。</font><br>\n
signal	<h3>signal</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>信号, 暗号<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Signals are made with flags or lamps.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 用旗或灯传递信号。</font><br>(无线电或电视所传送的)讯号, 讯息, 图像<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We live too far from the city to get a strong television signal.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们住的地方离城里太远, 不能收到清晰的电视图像。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>发信号; 用信号传达; 用信号通讯<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is signaling.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她正在发送信号。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The submarine signaled for help.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 潜水艇发出求救的信号。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She signaled the advance.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她发出信号前进。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She signaled that he was about to turn left.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她打手势表示他就要转到左面去了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They signaled which way one is going to turn.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们打信号示意走哪一条路。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He signaled a message to his brother.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他用信号向他哥哥发信息。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He signaled the waiter to bring the menu.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他作手势要侍者拿菜单来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The conductor signaled the orchestra to rise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 指挥打手势让乐队起立。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Tom signaled his friend which way to go.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 汤姆示意他的朋友走哪条路。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>明显的, (非常)显著的, 非凡的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is a signal failure.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是明显的失败。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp People speak of Mark Twain as a signal humourous writer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 人们称马克·吐温为杰出的幽默作家。</font><br>\n
silence	<h3>silence</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>寂静; 无声<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Now and then a bird's song broke in upon the silence of the wood.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 鸟鸣声不时打破林中的寂静。</font><br>沉默<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What is the reason for your long silence?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你长时间沉默的原因是什么?</font><br>无音信, 失去联系<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Forgive me for my long silence.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请原谅我好久没给你写信。</font><br>寂静[沉默, 无音信]的时刻[期间]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let's observe a minute's silence in memory of the dead.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 让我们为死者静默一分钟。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>使安静, 使沉默<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The arrival of the teacher silenced the class.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 教师的到来使全班安静下来。</font><br>\n
silent	<h3>silent</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>寂静的; 无声的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The cat moved on silent feet.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那只猫无声地走动着。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The old house was quite silent.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这间旧房子非常肃静。</font><br>沉默的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is a silent type.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是个沉默型的人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Gradually he became silent.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 渐渐地他变得沉默寡言了。</font><br>不发音的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The “e” in “ time” is a silent letter.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp time中的e不发音。</font><br>\n

till	<h3>till</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>conj.</i></font><br>直到…时(为止)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Please wait for me till I come back.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请等我回来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I sat up till she came back.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我一直坐到她回来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I waited till they should return.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我一直等到他们回来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He will wait till I arrive.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他将等到我来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He had hardly reached the station till the train arrived.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他刚到火车站, 火车就进站了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示时间)直到(某一时刻)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They talked till dawn.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们一直谈到天明。</font><br>(表示时间)直到(发生某事)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It was not till 11 o'clock that he came back last night.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 昨晚直到11点他才回来。</font><br>\n

understanding	<h3>understanding</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>了解; 相互理解, 谅解; (非正式)协议<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This argument aimed at the understanding rather than the emotions.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这场辩论针对的是理解而不是感情。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We have reached an understanding with them.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们和他们达成了协议。</font><br>理解(力); 认识<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His understanding of English is good.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他对英语的理解力很好。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We must have a clear understanding of the problem.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们对这一问题必须有一个清醒的认识。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>体谅的; 谅解的; 通情达理的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The youth was fortunate in having understanding parents.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个青年有通情达理的父母, 真幸运。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Because she is understanding, people around her confide in her.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 因为她通情达理, 周围的人都相信她。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Try to be understanding.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请多谅解。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She was understanding about what happened.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她了解所有发生的事。</font><br>\n

yield	<h3>yield</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>生产, 出产, 带来<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This land yields well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这块土地产量高。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This old tree still yields apples every year.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这棵老树仍然每年结苹果。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A cow will yield several gallons of milk each day.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 一头母牛每天产几加仑的牛奶。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His business yields big profits.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的企业获利大。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This article yield-ed us great profit.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这东西给我们带来了很大的收益。</font><br>屈服, 放弃; 不再反对, 让出<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We shall never yield.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们绝不投降。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The terrorists have yielded two of their hostages.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 恐怖分子交出了两名人质。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We were forced to yield the city.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们被迫放弃这座城市。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She yielded me her books.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她把书让给了我。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She yielded her property to me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她把她的财产让给我了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>变形, 折断, 塌陷<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The shelf is beginning to yield under that heavy weight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 架子受不了那重量, 开始塌下去了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>产量, 收益<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All these have helped raise farm yields steadily.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 所有这些都有助于农业产量的稳步提高。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The yields on his shares have increased in this year.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 今年他的股票红利增加了。</font><br>\n

yours	<h3>yours</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>你(们)的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This book is yours, not mine.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这本书是你的, 不是我的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is my pen, and yours is on the table.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是我的钢笔, 你的在桌子上。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Our school is not as big as yours.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们的学校没有你们的大。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You said he was a friend of yours.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你说过他是你的一个朋友。</font><br>\n
zone	<h3>zone</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>(划分出来的)地区, 区域, 地带<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Do not enter the danger zone!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 切勿进入危险区！</font><br>气候带<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>将…划分<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They zoned the house into sleeping, sitting and dining rooms.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们将房子区分成卧室、客厅和餐厅。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This small town has been zoned as a shopping area.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个小镇已划作商业区。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The whole hospital area has been zoned off until the infection is under control.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在这种传染病得到控制以前, 整个医院已同外界隔离。</font><br>\n
